I recommend that you supplement CoQ10 which is depleted by all statins and is necessary for optimal energy production at a cellular level. Taking a high quality omega 3 as prescribed will also aid lowering cardiac risk.

Overview Notes: Exercise and Diet: Eating a more diverse array of colourful fruits and vegetables will help to optimise how you are feeling and lower inflammatory risk. While your cardio exercise is excellent, resistance training is essential for building bone and preventing aches and pains.

Overview Notes: Cholesterol:. Your Lipogram is within acceptable range for your risk profile. I recommend that you supplement CoQ10 which is depleted by all statins and is necessary for optimal energy production at a cellular level. Taking a high quality omega 3 as prescribed will also aid lowering cardiac risk.

Men's Health Recommendations: -Prostate specific antigen is within normal limits. If the changes to your urinary habits persist please see a urologist.
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Cholesterol:. Your Lipogram is within acceptable range for your risk profile. I recommend that you supplement CoQ10 which is depleted by all statins and is necessary for optimal energy production at a cellular level. Taking a high quality omega 3 as prescribed will also aid lowering cardiac risk.

Comment Key: VitalsNote
Comment Value: Fit with a need for resistance and corset training.
Special Investigation Notes: All normal
